# Atlas Leap V2
A 3D printable adapter that lets you mount a Herman Miller Atlas headrest to a Steelcase Leap V2 chair without making any intrusive changes to you Leap chair.



# Printing instructions:
 V1 (this version is superseded by V2):
 - Infill: 20%-30%
 - Layer height: 0.2mm
 - Supports: no 

V2 (the v2 design has a bottom clamp that can be screwed in with 4 screws, the 2 bottom ones being optional):
- Infill: 20%-30%
- Layer height: 0.2m
- Supports: yes
- Screws: 4x(2 optional) M6x40mm countersunk phillips screws

I'm done improving on the design, but for those of you that wish to further tinker with it, I've included a .step file that can be easily imported and modified with a 3D modelling software like Fusion 360.
